Rides the same Run-feature gate as Java/Python ‚Äî **no `make`-on-PATH detection** (a missing `make` surfaces as a clear `onError` in the Run console). **Shebang language detection** (pure/unit-tested **`editor/Shebang`**): when a file's extension resolves to plaintext, `EditorBuffer.maybeApplyShebang` (run at the top of `recomputeRun`) promotes it to the language named by a first-line interpreter shebang ‚Äî direct path (`#!/bin/bash`), `env` lookup (`#!/usr/bin/env python3`), or `env -S` with args ‚Äî reducing the interpreter to its basename (version-stripped: `python3.12`‚Üípython), mapping it to a **representative extension**, and resolving language+grammar through the normal `forFileName("shebang.<ext>")` path so highlighting/folding/run/LSP all follow (shell for bash/zsh/sh/dash/ksh/‚Ä¶, python, javascript for node, typescript for deno/bun/ts-node/tsx, ruby, php, lua, groovy, powershell). A `java --source N` shebang ‚Üí Java compact source: `getShebangJavaSource()` widens `recomputeRun`'s compact-source branch (via `CompactSource.hasTopLevelMain`, no `.java` needed) and feeds `RunCoordinator.buildRunCommand` a `java --source N <file>` argv (an extensionless file needs the flag). It never overrides a real extension or the user's status-bar language pick (`setLanguageOverride` sets a `languageUserOverride` guard). *(jdtls keys off `.java`, so an extensionless Java shebang file gets highlighting/run but likely no jdtls LSP; python/shell LSP work since the languageId is sent explicitly. The tab file-icon stays generic ‚Äî it's filename-based.)* `EditorBuffer.recomputeRun` caches `runnable`/`runLine` (recomputed on load, Save-As, and the debounced 150 ms edit pulse; skipped for large files), fires `onRunnableChanged`, and exposes `isRunnable()`/`isPython()`/`isShell()` + `setRunHandler` (‚Üí controller `runActiveFile`). **Gutter affordance**: `FoldManager.setRunHooks(enabled, isRunLine, onRun)` reserves a fixed `RUN_SLOT_WIDTH` slot **just left of the line number, only while runnable** (so other files' gutters are unaffected and the glyph never shifts text), drawing a clickable green play glyph (`FoldManager.runGlyph()`, `.run-marker`, right-aligned) on the entry line; the same glyph is the **right-click "Run File"** item. **`run/RunService.run(file, argv, listener)`** streams a launched program ‚Äî `[java, <file>]` (JDK source-file launcher; needs JDK 25 on PATH, no `--enable-preview` since JEP 512 is final in 25), `[python3, <file>]`, or `[bash, <file>]` (the controller picks by `isPython()`/`isShell()`, else java) ‚Äî via `ProcessBuilder` reusing `ProcessRunner.resolveExecutable`/`applyStandardEnv`, two daemon reader threads posting stdout/stderr to the FX thread (generation-guarded), `stop()` kills it; **`sendInput(line)`** writes one line to the process's stdin off-thread (so `IO.readln`-style console programs work) and **`detectJavaMajor(cb)`** probes `java -version` once (cached; the pure `javaMajorOf` parse handles the legacy `1.8` scheme ‚Äî tested) so `runActiveFile` can **preflight** a java run and report a clear "needs JDK 25 ‚Äî found Java N" instead of a cryptic launcher error. **Program arguments**: per-file args persist in `WorkspaceState.programArgs` (path ‚Üí raw string; additive field), tokenized by the pure/unit-tested **`run/ProgramArgs.tokenize`** (quote-aware) and appended to the run argv; **the same stored args feed debug launches** (`DapManager.setProgramArgs` before `startLaunch` ‚Äî sticky across `restart()`; `LaunchConfig.launch` already took java args, `program(...)` gained an args overload for debugpy/js-debug). Commands `file.runWithArgs` (prompt pre-filled via `promptText`, saved per file) and `run.rerun` (re-runs the last file+argv). **Clickable stack traces**: the pure/unit-tested **`run/StackTraceLinks.parse(line)`** recognizes Java (`(File.java:12)`), Python (`File "/path", line N`), and Node (`/path/x.js:12:5`) frames; double-clicking such a console line (the shared `RunPanel.installLinkClicks`, also installed on the Debug console) resolves the file (absolute path ‚Üí direct; bare Java name ‚Üí open tabs ‚Üí the run file's dir ‚Üí the project root) and jumps via `openAndGoto`. **jdtls noise filter**: for a compact buffer (`language==java && isRunnable()`), `onLspDiagnostics` drops implicit-class complaints from a server whose compliance predates JDK 25 (pure `MainController.isCompactSourceNoise`, tested) while real errors still surface. Bundled `snippets/java.json` gained `cmain` (compact main skeleton) + `ioprintln`/`ioreadln` (JEP 512 final dropped the implicit static IO import, so bodies use `IO.println`). **`ui/RunPanel`** (a `ToolWindowContent`; tool id `run`, `Side.BOTTOM`, `tool.run`/`M-9`, `Icons.run()`) is a read-only monospace console (output capped) with Stop/Clear + a run-state header. The window wiring lives in **`ui/RunCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` feature-coordinator pattern ‚Äî owns the `RunService` + the `RunPanel`, the `runActiveFile`/`rerunLast`/`launchRun`/`buildRunCommand`/`stopRun` flow + the `lastRun` file/argv, reaching the window via the shared host plus an `Ops` extension for open-tool-window / save-buffer / program-args get+set / stack-trace-link jump): `runActiveFile` saves first (dirty ‚Üí save; untitled ‚Üí Save-As), opens the Run window, then streams. `MainController` keeps the `ToolWindow` (built with `runCoordinator.panel()`), `updateRunButton` (gates the Run stripe on `isRunnable()`), the `programArgsFor` helper (shared with debug launches), and the shared `openRunLink` stack-trace resolver (which reuses `runCoordinator.lastRunDir()`); `buffer.setRunHandler` and the `file.run`/`run.*` commands delegate to the coordinator. Commands `file.run` (`C-c r`), `run.stop`, `run.clear` (`RunPanel.clearConsole`), `tool.run` (`M-9`) ‚Äî palette-discoverable, localized in all six catalogs. **No new Maven dependency / `module-info` change** (`com.editora.run` is internal to the module). *Deferred: running regular (non-compact) Java / other languages, a configurable run command per language, run configurations.*
- `http/` ‚Äî **HTTP Client for `.http`/`.rest` files** (on by default, gated by `Settings.httpClientSupport`). Runs requests with the **built-in JDK `java.net.http.HttpClient`** (no external tool ‚Äî `ijhttp` was tried first but it's a CI test-runner: slow JVM startup + a progress report instead of the response body). **`http/HttpFile`** (pure, unit-tested) parses a file into `Request{startLine,endLine,method,url,name,block}` (requests split on `###`) and one request's `block` into `Parsed{method,url,List<String[]> headers,body,‚Ä¶,warning}` (`parseRequest`; merges indented URL-continuation lines, stops the body at a `>`/`<>` response-handler line). A header line is only taken as a header when its name is a valid RFC 7230 field-name token (`isHeaderFieldName`); a non-blank line in the header block that isn't ‚Äî almost always a **request body written without the blank line before it** (a common typo where a colon-bearing body like `{"a": 1}` used to be split into a bogus header and the POST sent empty) ‚Äî sets `Parsed.warning` instead, which `HttpClientService` threads into `HttpResult.warnings` so it renders atop the report. No body is sent without the blank separator (spec-compliant, per the JetBrains `.http` convention) rather than guessing where the body starts (#441). `requestIndexAt(text,line)` maps a clicked line; `fileVariablePairs(text)` returns the `@name = value` declarations. **`http/HttpEnv`** (pure) reads environment names + one environment's variable map from `http-client.env.json`. **`http/HttpVars`** (pure, unit-tested) substitutes `{{name}}` from a resolved map + dynamic built-ins (`{{$uuid}}`/`{{$timestamp}}`/`{{$randomInt}}`/`{{$isoTimestamp}}`); `resolve(env, fileVars, clock)` layers the file's `@vars` over the env vars (each resolved against the accumulating map). **`http/HttpClientService`** (UI fa√ßade, daemon executor + `Platform.runLater`) executes a `Parsed` request via the shared `HttpClient` (`run`, and `runAll` for the whole file) ‚Äî substitutes url/headers/body, times it, returns an **`HttpResult`** (status/headers/body/contentType/elapsed/size/error/**warnings**). **`HttpHeaders.partition`** (pure) prepares the headers: it **trims every value** (spec-safe OWS strip ‚Äî a token pasted with a trailing `\r\n` the JDK would reject is now sent, not silently dropped; only `Authorization` was trimmed before, via `HttpAuth.normalizeHeaders`) and **surfaces** any header still un-sendable (a restricted name, or an embedded control char = header-injection) as an `HttpResult.warnings` line atop the report, instead of the old silent `catch (IllegalArgumentException)` skip that turned a dropped auth header into a mystery `401`. **`http/HttpResponseFormat`** (pure, unit-tested) renders a readable report: status line + headers + blank + body (**pretty-printed JSON** by content type) + a `status ¬∑ ms ¬∑ size` footer. **Gutter ‚ñ∂ per request**: `.http` reuses the run-slot ‚Äî `FoldManager.setRunHooks`'s `onRun` was generalized from `Runnable` to `IntConsumer onRunLine` (the clicked line); `EditorBuffer.recomputeRun` marks **every** request start line runnable for an http buffer (`isHttpFile()` + `setHttpEnabled`, a gate *separate* from the LSP-gated `setRunEnabled`), and `onRunGlyph(line)` dispatches to the injected `httpRunHandler` (‚Üí `HttpClientCoordinator.runRequest`). Syntax highlighting via a bundled authored `grammars/http.tmLanguage.json` (`source.http`, ext `http`/`rest`; registered in `GrammarRegistry` `scopeToResource` **and** `mapExtensions` ‚Äî both needed; plus `LanguageRegistry`/`Commenter` `#` entries). **`ui/HttpClientPanel`** (a `ToolWindowContent`; id `http`, **`Side.RIGHT`**, `tool.http`/`M-0`, `Icons.httpClient()`) shows the rendered response in a read-only monospace area with an **environment `ComboBox`** (names from `HttpEnv`, persisted in `WorkspaceState.httpEnvironment`), **Save response** (FileChooser), and Clear. **Auto-show for `.http` buffers:** `MainController.applyHttpAutoToolWindow(buffer, httpActive)` (from `updateRunButton`, run on every tab switch) auto-opens the HTTP window when the active buffer is a `.http` file (feature on) and auto-hides it otherwise ‚Äî `setAvailable(false)` already closes it on leave, and showing it **displaces then restores** any other right-side window (`openRightWindowExcept` + the `httpDisplacedRight` field). A **manual** close is remembered per buffer in `httpUserClosed` (a weak-keyed `Set<EditorBuffer>`) so it isn't re-shown for that file until the user reopens it (a manual open / running a request clears it); an *automatic* close on leaving isn't remembered, so returning re-shows it. User-vs-auto is detected via `ToolWindowManager.setStateListener((tw,opened)->‚Ä¶)` (fired from `open`/`close`), guarded by the `httpAutoMutating` flag the controller wraps around its own programmatic open/close. **`ui/HttpClientCoordinator`** (extracted from `MainController` ‚Äî the shared-`CoordinatorHost` pattern plus a small `WindowOps` extension for the tool-window/tab/run-gating; `MainController` keeps the `ToolWindow` registration): `runRequest(buffer,line)` parses the request, builds the variable map (`httpVariables`: the selected env's public+private env-file vars overlaid with the file's `@vars`), runs it off-thread, renders the result into the panel; `applySupport()` (init + every settings apply) pushes `setHttpEnabled(on)` to each buffer + re-gates the tool window (no external detection); the commands no-op when off (`ifHttp`) and `http.*`/`tool.http` are filtered from the palette. Commands `http.runRequest` (run the request at the caret), `http.runFile` (all requests sequentially), `http.selectEnvironment`, `tool.http` (`M-0`). `Settings.httpClientSupport` (Settings ‚Üí **HTTP Client**, just an enable checkbox; schema 18‚Üí19 additive-identity). **`module-info` `requires java.net.http`** ‚Äî no new Maven dependency (env JSON uses the existing Jackson; the grammar rides `opens com.editora.grammars`). *Deferred: response-handler JS scripts (`> {% %}`) + cross-request captured variables (a request needing an earlier one's token can't run in isolation), request history, multipart/file bodies, a form/structured response viewer.*
- `web/` ‚Äî **HTML Live Preview** (on by default, gated by `Settings.htmlPreviewSupport`). A floating "open in browser" globe overlaid top-right of any `.html`/`.htm`/`.xhtml` editor (mirroring the Markdown preview toggle) opens the current file in a **detected desktop browser** over a tiny embedded HTTP server, with **live-as-you-type reload**. **`web/LivePreviewServer`** wraps one JDK `com.sun.net.httpserver.HttpServer` bound to `127.0.0.1:0` (**loopback only**, never the LAN). `setPreview(file, Supplier<String> liveText)` makes the file's parent dir the document root; the previewed file is served from the buffer's **live in-memory text** (so unsaved edits show), assets (CSS/JS/images) from disk; a `/__editora_livereload` **long-poll** endpoint holds the request until `bumpVersion()` advances a `volatile long` (or a ~25 s timeout), and a small **injected `<script>`** (spliced before `</body>`, appended if none) reloads the page on a `200`. Pure/unit-tested helpers: `injectReloadScript`, `contentType` (extension‚ÜíMIME), `safeResolve` (path-traversal guard rejecting escapes outside the doc root). A cached daemon thread pool backs it so held polls don't starve serving. **`web/Browsers`** (pure/unit-tested) detects installed browsers per-OS ‚Äî macOS app bundles (`Safari.app` always; `Google Chrome.app`/`Firefox.app`/`Microsoft Edge.app` in `/Applications` + `~/Applications`, launched `open -a`), Linux PATH binaries (via `ProcessRunner.resolveExecutable`, launched `[bin, url]`), Windows Program Files exes (`cmd /c start`) ‚Äî plus a **System Default** entry routed through `HostServices.showDocument`; the OS + filesystem/PATH probes are injected so detection + `launchArgv` are testable. **`web/HtmlPreviewService`** (UI-owned, the `MermaidService` idiom: single daemon executor + `Platform.runLater` + cached `detectBrowsers`) owns the one server per window; `preview(file, liveText, browser, cb)` (re)binds the doc root, launches the browser **detached** (fire-and-forget, so a foreground browser process can't stall the executor) or via the system opener, and posts a `Result`; `notifyChanged()` ‚Üí `bumpVersion()`; `stopServer()` (feature disabled) vs `shutdown()` (window close). **`EditorBuffer`** (editor pkg, no `ui` dep): `isHtml()`, an injected `setHtmlPreviewControl(Node)` overlaid via the same code-pane top-right anchoring as the Markdown toggle (`attachControlToCodePane` generalized to place either the markdown `viewModeControl` *or* the `htmlPreviewControl` ‚Äî mutually exclusive, a buffer is one or the other), and `setHtmlPreviewDirtyListener` fired from the **existing debounced** `multiPlainChanges` 250 ms pulse while `isHtml()` (no new per-keystroke work). **`ui/HtmlPreviewToggle`** (a `Button`, `Icons.htmlPreview()` globe, `.html-preview-toggle`) drops a `ContextMenu` of detected browsers (+ System Default) on click, **each menu item with its own recognizable glyph** (`HtmlPreviewToggle.iconFor(id)` ‚Üí `Icons.browserSafari/Chrome/Firefox/Edge` ‚Äî a Material compass for Safari + the Simple-Icons monochrome single-path logos for the rest; System Default / unknown falls back to the globe; Simple Icons is CC0, attributed in NOTICE). **`ui/HtmlPreviewCoordinator`** (a feature coordinator extracted from `MainController`, the `LogViewerCoordinator` pattern ‚Äî owns the `HtmlPreviewService` + the detected-browser list + the browser picker, and reaches the window only through a shared `CoordinatorHost` interface; `MainController` supplies an anonymous `Host` adapter and keeps one-line delegations, and a fake `Host` makes it unit-testable ‚Äî see `HtmlPreviewCoordinatorFxTest`): `applySupport()` (init + every settings apply, mirrors `applyMermaidSupport`) (un)attaches the globe on local HTML buffers + async-detects browsers, or `stopServer()`s when off; `ensureControl` gates on `isEnabled() && isHtml() && host.isLocalBuffer` (remote SFTP excluded ‚Äî the server reads sibling assets from disk); `previewActive` requires a saved file (so assets resolve), remembers the last-used browser in `Settings.htmlPreviewBrowser`; `onBufferEdited` reloads the served file on the debounced edit pulse; the `open`/`openIn` commands no-op when off (`ifEnabled`) and `htmlPreview.*` is palette-filtered. Commands (palette-only, no keymap binding ‚Äî like preview/print): `htmlPreview.open` (last-used/default browser), `htmlPreview.openIn` (`QuickOpen` browser picker), `view.toggleHtmlPreview` (master toggle ‚Üí `SettingsWindow.syncHtmlPreviewCheck`). `Settings.htmlPreviewSupport`/`htmlPreviewBrowser` (Settings ‚Üí **HTML Preview**, enable checkbox; schema 24‚Üí25 additive-identity). **`module-info` `requires jdk.httpserver`** ‚Äî **no new Maven dependency, no moditect** (a JDK module jlink bundles automatically); no `opens` (the last-used-browser is a plain `Settings` string). *Deferred: in-app WebView render (Editora ships no `javafx.web`; external browsers are the explicit design), remote (SFTP) HTML preview, multi-file concurrent previews (v1 serves one active file + its dir), a configurable server port, project-root document root.*
- `dap/` ‚Äî **Multi-language debugging (Debug Adapter Protocol)** for **Java**, **Python**, and **JavaScript (Node)**, off by default (gated by `Settings.debugSupport`). Three transports, abstracted in `dap/DapClient`: **Java** is **layered on the jdtls LSP session** (not a standalone server) ‚Äî jdtls is started with the Microsoft **java-debug** plugin jar in `initialize.initializationOptions.bundles`, which registers `vscode.java.*` debug commands; at debug time `LspManager.executeCommand(file, "vscode.java.startDebugSession")` returns a **TCP port** and `DapClient.connect(port, "java")` opens a socket. **Python** is **debugpy over stdio** ‚Äî `DapManager` spawns `<python> -m debugpy.adapter` and `DapClient.connectStdio(proc, "python")` wires DAP to the process's stdin/stdout. **JavaScript** is **vscode-js-debug over a socket** ‚Äî `DapManager` allocates a free port, spawns `node <dapDebugServer.js> <port>`, and `DapClient.connect(port, "pwa-node")` connects. All speak DAP via **`org.eclipse.lsp4j.debug`** (`DSPLauncher`). The standalone adapters' stderr is `Redirect.DISCARD`ed (undrained PIPE deadlocks, like the LSP servers), and `DapClient.dispose()` kills the adapter subprocess **tree** (descendants first, then root) so a wrapper script can't orphan the real adapter. **`dap/DapServerRegistry`** (pure, unit-tested) is the language‚Üíadapter spec: `java`‚Üí`Kind.JDTLS`, `python`‚Üí`Kind.STDIO` (launch `type="python"`, default interpreter `python3`, adapter args `-m debugpy.adapter`), `javascript`‚Üí`Kind.SOCKET` (launch `type="pwa-node"`, interpreter `node`); `languageIdsForDebug()`={java,python,javascript} gates the breakpoint gutter + debug commands; `interpreterArgv(lang, command)` tokenizes the configured interpreter (blank ‚áí default). The **LSP bridge** (`lsp/`, java only): `LanguageServerSession` gained an optional `initializationOptions` (jdtls gets `{"bundles":[<jar>]}` only when debugging is on) + `executeCommand`; `LspManager` gained `setDebugBundles`/`executeCommand`/`restartServer("java")` ‚Äî toggling debug **restarts jdtls** so it reloads with the bundle (via `restartServer` ‚Üí `shutdownServer`, whose scan prefix must agree with `LspManager.sessionKey`'s `SESSION_KEY_SEP` ‚Äî they silently didn't, so it was a no-op). **`dap/DebugAdapterLocator`** (pure, unit-tested) finds each adapter: `locate(...)` the java-debug jar (`com.microsoft.java.debug.plugin-*.jar` from a configured path / VS Code `vscjava.vscode-java-debug-*` / mason / `~/.editora[-dev]/plugins/dap/java/`, newest wins); `locateJsDebugServer(...)` the newest `dapDebugServer.js` (config path / `~/.editora[-dev]/plugins/dap/javascript/` / mason `js-debug-adapter` / VS Code `ms-vscode.js-debug-*`, by an embedded path version); `locateDebugpy(...)` a `PYTHONPATH` dir containing a `debugpy` package (config path / `~/.editora[-dev]/plugins/dap/python/`, empty ‚áí rely on the interpreter importing debugpy). **`dap/DapClient`** (mirrors `LanguageServerSession`) runs the DAP handshake (`initialize` with the per-transport `adapterId` ‚Üí on the `initialized` event fire `setBreakpoints`/`setExceptionBreakpoints`/`configurationDone` **without `.join()`** ‚Äî that callback runs on the reader thread, so blocking deadlocks). `initialized` is the **only** reader of `exceptionFilters`, so once it has fired (tracked by `configured`) a later `setExceptionFilters` must put the request on the wire **itself** ‚Äî otherwise toggling exception breakpoints mid-session writes a field nothing will read again and silently does nothing while the UI reports success., `launch`/`attach`, and the control + inspection requests; events arrive on the launcher thread and a `Host` (DapManager) marshals to FX. **`dap/DapManager`** (UI facade, mirrors `LspManager`+`RunService`) owns the **single** session and dispatches `startLaunch(file, language, picker)`: `java` ‚Üí the jdtls flow (`resolveMainClass` ‚Üí pick ‚Üí `resolveClasspath` ‚Üí `resolveJavaExecutable` ‚Üí `startDebugSession` ‚Üí connect ‚Üí `launch`, with a `compileAndLaunch` javac fallback for loose files); `python`/`javascript` ‚Üí `startProgram` (snapshot breakpoints on FX, then off-thread spawn the adapter + connect + `launch`). `configure(enabled, javaPluginPath, pythonEnabled, pythonCommand, jsEnabled, jsPath)` resolves all three adapter locations synchronously; `detectPython`/`detectJs` probe `python -c "import debugpy"` / `node --version` off-thread and cache `isLanguageAvailable(lang)`. It exposes neutral records (`dap/DapModels`) so `ui`/`editor` never import lsp4j.debug; jdtls's untyped `executeCommand` results (gson `JsonElement`s) are parsed with gson (`module-info` `requires com.google.gson` + `opens com.editora.dap`). **`dap/LaunchConfig`** (pure, unit-tested) shapes the DAP arg maps: `launch` (java mainClass+classpath), `attach` (java JVM host:port ‚Äî **attach stays Java-only**), and `program(type, program, cwd, runtimeExecutable, stopOnEntry)` for python/js (the interpreter goes under `python` for python, `runtimeExecutable` for node). **Both pass program args as the argv array, never a joined string** ‚Äî `ProgramArgs.tokenize` already resolved the user's quoting, so re-joining on a space undoes it (`"hello world" second` ‚Üí 3 args to `main()` while Run passes 2). **Breakpoints** (`config/Breakpoint` + per-project `config/BreakpointStore` in `breakpoints.json`, `ConfigSchema.BREAKPOINTS`; `editor/BreakpointManager` mirrors `BookmarkManager`, `shift`/`reanchor` pure + unit-tested ‚Äî **`reanchor` resolves each marker against the lines not already claimed**, walking the list in stored-line order: it rebuilds a *line-keyed map*, so two markers landing on one line silently `put`-drop one and `restore`'s self-heal then **persists** the loss ‚Äî trivially hit by two breakpoints on adjacent identical lines (`});`/`});`) plus any external edit. The same fix is in `BookmarkManager.reanchor`, where the dropped bookmark took its **note** with it) show in a **leftmost gutter strip** (`FoldManager.setBreakpointHooks` reserves `BREAKPOINT_SLOT_WIDTH` only while debug is on **and the buffer's language is debuggable** ‚Äî java/python/javascript, via `DebugCoordinator.isDebuggableBuffer`; clicking toggles a bp + consumes so it never collides with the bookmark gutter click; red dot `.breakpoint-marker`, amber/blue/hollow for conditional/logpoint/disabled). `EditorBuffer` mirrors the bookmark API + a **current-execution-line** (`setExecutionLine`/`clearExecutionLine`, `.exec-line`). **`ui/DebugPanel`** (a `ToolWindowContent`, id `debug`, `Side.BOTTOM`, `tool.debug`/`M-g d`, `Icons.debug()`) is **IntelliJ-styled**: an icon-only grouped toolbar (resume/pause/stop/restart | step over/into/out/run-to-cursor, full titles in tooltips; the state + session file right-aligned), a **thread `ComboBox`** over the call-stack `ListView` (rich `name:line, File` `TextFlow` cells), a lazy variables `TreeView` with **type-colored values** (`record VarRow(name,value,type,ref,parentRef,Kind {SCOPE,VARIABLE,WATCH,ADD_WATCH})`; the pure, unit-tested **`ui/DebugValues`** classifies a rendered value STRING/NUMBER/BOOLEAN/NULL/OTHER ‚Üí `.debug-val-*` CSS), and an always-visible console with an evaluate REPL. **Watches** are merged into the variables tree IntelliJ-style: a fixed top "Watches" node above the scopes + a trailing "+ Add watch‚Ä¶" row; add/edit/remove via the tree context menu or double-click, prompting through the injected `OverlayInput.Prompt` (`DebugPanel.setPrompt`); each watch evaluates per stop/frame-select with context `"watch"` via `DapClient.evaluateFull` ‚Üí `DapModels.EvalResult(result, variablesReference, type)` (expandable when structured); the expression list persists in **`WorkspaceState.debugWatches`** (additive field; restored at startup + on project switch, saved via `setOnWatchesChanged`). **Set Value**: context-menu "Set Value‚Ä¶" / F2 / double-click on a leaf variable row ‚Üí prompt pre-filled with the current value ‚Üí `DapManager.setVariable` on the row's `parentRef`, updating the row in place + re-evaluating watches. **The whole DAP integration lives in `ui/DebugCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` feature-coordinator pattern ‚Äî owns the `DebugPanel`, breakpoint persistence + gutter gating, the DAP event sink (`dapListener`) + panel actions (`debugActions`), the inline-values/hover/execution-line editor surfaces (`applyInlineValues`/`highlightFrame`), the start/attach/step/run-to-cursor/jump flows, `wireBuffer` (the per-buffer breakpoint-gutter + change/hover hooks), and the `debug.toggleAdapter`/`debug.setAdapterPath` pickers; reaches the window via the shared host plus an `Ops` extension for the Debug tool-window open/toggle/availability, the status-bar debug segment + loading bar, save-buffer, program-args (shared with Run), the stack-trace-link jump, open-path, buffer-for-path, the debug-watches workspace state, and the `breakpoints.json` map). The **`DapManager` stays a `MainController` field** (built on `lspManager`; `SettingsWindow` + window-dispose reach it) and is passed to the coordinator ‚Äî mirroring the `lspManager`/`LspCoordinator` split; since Java debugging layers on the jdtls session, the coordinator also takes the `lspManager` + `LspCoordinator` (its `debugEffectiveFor("java")` reads `lspCoordinator.serverEnabled("java")`/`isServerAvailable("java")`; `applySupport` pushes the java-debug bundle + re-gates via `lspCoordinator.applyGating()`). `MainController` keeps the Debug `ToolWindow` (built with `debugCoordinator.panel()`), `isLocalBuffer`, the shared `programArgsFor`/`openRunLink`/`save` helpers, and the `debug.*` command registrations (delegating to the coordinator). **`DebugCoordinator`**: `applySupport()` configures all three adapters, pushes the java bundle into LSP (restart jdtls when changed), async-detects python/js (re-gating on each result), gates each buffer's breakpoint gutter via `debugSupportEnabled() && isDebuggableBuffer(b)`, and `setAvailable`s the Debug window; `debugEffectiveFor(language)` gates start (java = `lspSupport && javaLspEnabled && jdtls + plugin found`; python = `pythonDebugEnabled && debugpy detected`; js = `jsDebugEnabled && js-debug + node detected`); `debugStart()` reads the active buffer's language and dispatches; `ifDebug(...)` no-ops the commands when off (palette-filtered); persist/restore breakpoints on save/open. **Pause** (`DapClient.pause` ‚Üí the `stopped` event flows through the normal path; enabled only while RUNNING) and **Run to Cursor** (`DapManager.runToCursor`: the pure, unit-tested `withTempLine` merges a temporary breakpoint into the file's set ‚Üí `sendSetBreakpoints` ‚Üí resume; the temp set is re-sent clean on the next stop/termination) complement the step commands. **Jump to Line** (the IntelliJ plugin's move-the-execution-pointer): DAP `gotoTargets`/`goto`, **capability-gated** via the stored `initialize` `Capabilities` (`DapClient.supportsGotoTargets`) ‚Äî debugpy supports it, java-debug/js-debug don't (the command reports `status.debug.jumpUnsupported`); `DapManager.jumpToLine` teleports the suspended thread to the caret line *without executing* the code in between, and the adapter's `stopped(reason=goto)` refreshes everything. **Editor surfaces while suspended** (IntelliJ's inline values + value popup): on each stop/frame-select the controller fetches the selected frame's first non-expensive scope (capped at `MAX_INLINE_VALUES`) and pushes a name‚Üívalue map to the frame's file buffer ‚Äî **`editor/InlineValuesOverlay`** (a mouse-transparent `Canvas` mirroring `WhitespaceOverlay`: visible paragraphs only, coalesced per pulse, 1√ó1 when inactive) paints grey-italic `name: value` annotations after each visible line that mentions a frame variable (pure, unit-tested **`editor/DebugIdentifiers.matchesIn`**); hovering an identifier evaluates it with DAP context `"hover"` (`DebugIdentifiers.wordAt` ‚Üí the injected `EditorBuffer.setDebugHoverEvaluator` ‚Üí `DapManager.evaluateHover`, which delivers null on failure so non-variables show nothing) in a `.debug-value-tooltip`; both are gated by `setDebugHoverActive`/`setInlineValues(null)` flipped on suspend/resume, so there is zero editor hot-path cost outside a paused session. Commands (all `ifDebug`-gated): `debug.start` (`C-c C-d d`, = continue when suspended) / `debug.continue`/`stepOver`/`stepInto`/`stepOut` / `debug.pause` (`C-c C-d p`) / `debug.runToCursor` (`C-c C-d u`) / `debug.jumpToLine` (`C-c C-d j`) / `debug.stop` / `debug.restart` / `debug.attach` (Java only) / `debug.toggleBreakpoint` (`C-c C-b`) / `debug.editBreakpoint` (a 3-field `OverlayInput` form ‚Äî condition / log message / enabled; a log message makes it a **logpoint**: the adapter logs and never suspends. `BreakpointManager.setLogMessage`/`setEnabled` had **zero callers** before, so both states were built-but-unreachable and the gutter's logpoint/disabled glyphs were dead) / `debug.toggleExceptionBreakpoints` / `tool.debug` (`M-g d`). The panel's data-inspection actions are also palette commands: `debug.evaluate` (open the Debug console + focus the eval field via `DebugPanel.focusEvaluate`), `debug.addWatch` (`DebugPanel.addWatch`), `debug.setValue` (`DebugPanel.setSelectedValue`). Settings ‚Üí **Debugging** page is **data-driven** (`SettingsWindow.debugAdapterUis()`, mirroring the LSP page): a master enable + a per-language row group (Java/Python/JavaScript) ‚Äî Python/JS each an enable checkbox + command/path field, Java a plugin-path field (no enable ‚Äî gated by the Java LSP server) ‚Äî each with a live green/red found status (`refreshDebugStatus` ‚Üí the locators + `dapManager.detectPython/detectJs` probes). `Settings.debugSupport`/`javaDebugPluginPath`/`pythonDebugEnabled`/`pythonDebugCommand`/`jsDebugEnabled`/`jsDebugPath` (schema 15‚Üí16 additive-identity). **Adapter acquisition**: never bundled ‚Äî `scripts/install-java-debug.sh` (java-debug jar from Open VSX), `scripts/install-debugpy.sh` (`pip install --target ‚Ä¶/plugins/dap/python debugpy`), `scripts/install-js-debug.sh` (vscode-js-debug release ‚Üí `‚Ä¶/plugins/dap/javascript/js-debug/src/dapDebugServer.js`); all honor `EDITORA_CONFIG_DIR` for `--dev`. **Dependency**: `org.eclipse.lsp4j.debug` (same version as lsp4j; moditect-patched + signed-jar-unsigned in `dist`); **no new dependency / `module-info` change** for python/js (debugpy/js-debug are external, user-installed, driven over stdio/socket; node/python come from the augmented PATH). *Deferred: browser/Chrome JS debugging, TypeScript source-map debugging, Python/JS attach (remote), more languages (Go delve, Ruby) via the registry, hit-count/data breakpoints, hot code replace, sending a **closed** file's breakpoints to the adapter (`DebugCoordinator.collectBreakpoints` walks open buffers only, so a breakpoint in a closed file is saved + restored on reopen but never armed), run/debug configurations, multi-session tabs, smart step-into, drop frame, the Jump-to-Line gutter-arrow drag affordance.*
- `install/` ‚Äî **In-app install of language support** (LSP server + DAP adapter for Java/Python/JS, plus the Mermaid CLI), cross-platform (macOS/Linux/Windows), the Java path the bash `scripts/install-*.sh` used to be. Pure **`InstallCatalog`** (java.base only, unit-tested) maps a `Lang` (JAVA/PYTHON/JAVASCRIPT/MERMAID) ‚Üí an ordered `Step` list (`Kind` NPM_GLOBAL/PIP_TARGET/VSIX/TARBALL + its prereqs + dest), with the pure URL/argv helpers (`openVsxLatestUrl`, `JDTLS_TARBALL_URL`, `JS_DEBUG_RELEASES_API`, `npmInstallGlobalArgv`/`pipInstallTargetArgv`/`tarExtractArgv`, `firstMatch` for asset-URL extraction, `forBufferLanguage`). Recipes: **pyright**/**typescript-language-server**/**mmdc** = `npm i -g` (then `npx puppeteer browsers install chrome-headless-shell` from mmdc's dir, version-matched, so the headless Chrome it renders with is present ‚Äî `Kind.PUPPETEER_BROWSER`) (global); **debugpy** = `pip install --target <config>/plugins/dap/python`; **java-debug** = Open VSX `.vsix` (a ZIP) ‚Üí reuse `plugin/Unzip` ‚Üí `<config>/plugins/dap/java`; **jdtls** = Eclipse JDT-LS `.tar.gz` ‚Üí system `tar` ‚Üí `<config>/plugins/lsp/java` (then `Settings.javaLspCommand` ‚Üê `bin/jdtls`, the dir `ProcessRunner.EXTRA_PATH_DIRS` already anticipates); **js-debug** = GitHub release `.tar.gz` ‚Üí system `tar` ‚Üí `<config>/plugins/dap/javascript`. **`InstallService`** (the `GitService`/`MermaidService` idiom: one daemon executor + `Platform.runLater`) runs the steps off-thread reusing `ProcessRunner.run/resolveExecutable` (npm/pip/tar; Windows `.cmd`/`.exe` resolution + augmented PATH so a GUI-launched app finds them), `PluginRegistry.readCapped`+`isHttps` over `java.net.http` for bounded HTTPS downloads, and `Unzip.extract` for the vsix; `detectPrereqs` probes npm/python/tar on PATH. **`ui/InstallCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` pattern + a small `Ops` for config-dir / per-feature availability reads / re-detect): `installSupport(lang)` filters to the *missing* tools (per the existing `LspCoordinator.isServerAvailable`/`DapManager.isLanguageAvailable`/`MermaidCoordinator.mmdcAvailable` detectors), checks prereqs first (reports a missing Node/Python/tar instead of installing it ‚Äî Editora never installs runtimes), runs them, then `reapplyToolSupport()` (`LspManager.invalidateDetection()` + `LspCoordinator`/`DebugCoordinator`/`MermaidCoordinator` `applySupport()` + persist) so the tools activate **without a restart**. Palette commands `install.javaSupport`/`pythonSupport`/`jsSupport`/`mermaidSupport`. **Settings ‚Üí Language Servers** rows (java/python/typescript) and the **Mermaid** page also carry an **Install‚Ä¶** button (`SettingsWindow.setInstallActions` injected with a language-key consumer ‚Üí `installSupport`; tracked in `installButtons`, flipped to "Installed"/disabled by `updateInstallButton` from the existing `refreshLspStatus`/`refreshMermaidStatus` detect callbacks; `MainController`'s `reapplyToolSupport` calls `SettingsWindow.refreshDetectionStatus()` after an install so it updates live ‚Äî the JS row installs the LSP **and** js-debug, so the Debugger page needs no separate button). **In-editor install banner:** `EditorBuffer.getNode()`'s `BorderPane` top stacks (in a `VBox`, via `refreshTopBars`) a generic `.lsp-install-bar` (built lazily like `buildViewModeBar`; toolkit-only `setInstallPrompt(message, actionLabel, onInstall, onDismiss)` + `showInstallBar`/`setInstallBarBusy`, so `editor` stays decoupled) **above** the existing `.view-mode-bar`. `MainController.maybeOfferInstall(buffer)` (run on tab switch / after an install / on `reapplyAfterSharedSettingsChange`) shows it per `shouldOfferInstall`: the buffer's language has an installer, the relevant feature is **on** but its server/CLI is **confirmed missing** (`lspEnabled() && lspCoordinator.isServerMissing(...)` ‚Äî tri-state, *probed-and-absent* not merely pending; or `mermaid.isEnabled() && mmdcDetected() && !mmdcAvailable()`), no live LSP session is already serving the file (`!lspCoordinator.isManaged(path)`), the user hasn't dismissed it (a `WeakHashMap` `installDismissed`, mirroring `httpUserClosed`), it's a local buffer, and the master nudge `Settings.lspInstallPrompts` (default on, schema 44‚Üí45 additive; Settings ‚Üí Language Servers checkbox + `view.toggleInstallPrompts`) is on. **Install** runs `installCoordinator.installSupport(lang, ok‚Üí‚Ä¶)` (the callback overload spins the banner + hides on success); **Not now** dismisses for that buffer. The banner re-evaluates when LSP detection settles (`LspCoordinator.applyGating` ‚Üí `Ops.onDetectionSettled` ‚Üí `maybeOfferInstall`), so a late-starting server hides it without a tab switch. Downloads are HTTPS-only + capped; `Unzip` keeps its zip-slip/size guards; **no new Maven dependency / `module-info` change** (`install` is internal). **More LSP servers (server-id-centric):** beyond the 4 `Lang` bundles, `InstallCatalog.installableServerIds()` + `serverInstall(serverId)` describe the **LSP-only** servers (no DAP) keyed by their `LspServerRegistry` server id; `InstallCoordinator.installServer(serverId[, cb])` installs one (filters on `lspAvailable(serverId)`, prereq-checks, runs, re-detects). The Settings ‚Üí Language Servers rows get an **Install‚Ä¶** button for any `installableServerIds()` entry (`SettingsWindow.setInstallServerActions`), the editor banner offers them via `LspServerRegistry.serverIdFor(language)` (in `MainController.maybeOfferInstall`'s server-id branch), and the palette `install.languageServer` picks any installable server (`QuickOpen` over `installableServerIds()`). The npm batch (needs Node): **json/html/css** (one package `vscode-langservers-extracted`), **bash**, **yaml**, **dockerfile** (`dockerfile-language-server-nodejs`), **toml** (`@taplo/cli`). The **toolchain batch** (`Kind.TOOL_COMMAND` ‚Äî argv carried in the `Step.npmPackages` field; runs via the language's own package manager, gated on that toolchain being on PATH via the new `Prereq` GO/RUBY/DOTNET/RUSTUP/COMPOSER): **go** (`go install ‚Ä¶/gopls@latest`), **sql** (`go install ‚Ä¶/sqls@latest`), **ruby** (`gem install ruby-lsp`), **csharp** (`dotnet tool install --global csharp-ls`), **rust** (`rustup component add rust-analyzer`), **php** (`composer global require phpactor/phpactor`). The **binary batch** (`Kind.ARCHIVE` + `InstallCatalog.archiveSpec(serverId)` ‚Üí an `ArchiveSpec{apiUrl, Map<Platform,assetSubstring>, binaryName, binaryPrefix, commandSuffix}`; `InstallService.installArchive` picks the asset for `currentPlatform()` (`platformKey`, pure/unit-tested), downloads it, extracts (zip via the new capped `Unzip.extract(...,maxEntry,maxTotal,maxEntries)` since clangd's binary dwarfs the plugin caps; `.tar.gz` via system `tar`), `findBinary`-walks the tree, `chmod +x`es it, and returns the path ‚Üí the coordinator persists it into that server's `Settings.<id>LspCommand` via `applyServerCommand`): **clangd** (clangd/clangd), **xml**/lemminx (redhat-developer/vscode-xml, binary prefix-matched `lemminx-‚Ä¶`), **kotlin** (fwcd/kotlin-language-server, single `server.zip`), **lua** (LuaLS, per-OS tar.gz/zip), **terraform** (releases.hashicorp.com via the HashiCorp releases API, command suffix ` serve`). All 21 LSP servers now have an installer. *Deferred: a keymap binding for the install commands.*
- `ai/` + `agent/` ‚Äî **AI features** (three Settings pages; all off by default). **This is the only feature that transmits the user's source code to a third party ‚Äî treat every change to it as security-relevant.** Two independent halves: (1) **direct API** ‚Äî `ui/AiCoordinator` (the `CoordinatorHost` pattern) drives `ai/AiService` (a generation-guarded facade over `ai/AiClient`, which speaks either dialect via the pure `ai/AiProvider`: **ANTHROPIC** = `x-api-key` to the Messages API, **OPENAI** = `Authorization: Bearer` to any OpenAI-compatible server ‚Äî its default endpoint is deliberately **plain-http loopback** (`http://127.0.0.1:1234`, LM Studio) because `requiresApiKey()` is false for local inference, so a blanket https rule would break the feature's primary path). `ai/AiRequests` builds the bodies (capped by `truncate` at 120k chars) ‚Äî it sends the **selection**, never the whole buffer, and no file path/name; `ai/SseParser`+`OpenAiSse` decode the stream; `ai/AiErrors` maps failures. Commands: commit-message-from-staged-diff, explain-selection (into a Markdown buffer), rewrite-selection (an undoable edit, re-verified against the original text before it lands), and **inline completion** (`Settings.aiInlineCompletion`, its own `AiService` so it can't cancel an explicit action) with the floating `editor/AiActionsBar`. (2) **ACP agent** ‚Äî `agent/AcpClient` runs an external agent process over stdio JSON-RPC (`agent/AcpJson`, `agent/AcpAgentRegistry`), driven by `ui/AgentCoordinator`+`AgentPanel`; it correctly `ProcessRegistry.track`s + `killTree`s the process and **drains stderr past the log cap** (the undrained-PIPE deadlock documented for LSP/DAP). Gated by `Settings.aiSupport` **&&** `aiEnabled` **&&** `!simpleModeActive()`. **Credential invariants ‚Äî do not regress these:** the key is **per-provider** ‚Äî `Settings.aiApiKey` holds the **Anthropic** key and `Settings.aiApiKeyOpenai` the **OpenAI-compatible** one, read via `Settings.getApiKeyFor(provider)`/`setApiKeyFor(provider, key)` ‚Äî because a single shared field silently sent one provider's key to the *other*'s (user-supplied) endpoint the moment you switched provider (#480; schema 77‚Üí78, `ConfigMigrations.splitAiApiKeyByProvider` moves an existing key onto `aiApiKeyOpenai` only when the saved provider was OpenAI, since Anthropic was the default and already lands in the right field). The Settings AI page's single key field shows/edits the *currently-selected* provider's key (the provider combo reloads it on switch, guarded by `loading`; the key field's listener writes to the combo's current provider). Both live in `settings.toml`, which `config/ConfigWriter` writes **owner-only (0600)** since the default umask left a billable credential world-readable in a 0755 config dir; and `AiCoordinator.effectiveKey(configured, provider, envKey)` (pure, unit-tested) **only** falls back to the `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` environment variable for the **ANTHROPIC** provider ‚Äî it is Anthropic's credential by name and is exported on most dev machines, so a provider-agnostic fallback shipped it as a bearer token to the OpenAI provider's user-supplied endpoint with the Settings field empty, on every inline-completion idle pause. `AiCoordinator.apiKey()` resolves `getApiKeyFor(provider())`, so each provider only ever sees its own configured key. **The key is never sent in cleartext to a remote host:** `AiClient` refuses (via `onError`/the check-string, **before dialing**) whenever a key would be attached to a **non-loopback `http://`** endpoint ‚Äî the pure/unit-tested `ai/AiEndpoints.isCleartextRemote(endpoint)` is true only when the scheme isn't https **and** the host isn't loopback (`localhost`/`127.0.0.0/8`/`::1`), so plain-http *loopback* (LM Studio/Ollama/vLLM, the intended local-inference path) and https are both allowed, and a keyless local server is unaffected (#481). A deceptive hostname that merely resolves to loopback (nip.io-style) is a remote host string and is refused ‚Äî we don't do DNS. **A hanging endpoint can't wedge the AI worker:** the streaming read's response timeout only bounds the wait for the *headers*, so an endpoint that returns `200` then writes nothing would block the read forever ‚Äî and since `AiService` runs on a **single-thread executor**, every later request would queue behind it permanently. `AiClient.stream` runs an **idle-read watchdog** (a shared daemon `ai-idle-watchdog` scheduler): each received line resets a `lastActivity` clock, and if no data arrives for `responseTimeout` the watchdog **closes the response stream** ‚Äî the only thing that unblocks a `readLine` already blocked mid-read (`cancel()` is polled *between* lines and can't) ‚Äî so the read fails fast and the worker returns to the queue. A healthy slow generation is untouched: Anthropic sends periodic ping events, so the clock keeps resetting (#482).
- `update/` ‚Äî **Update notifications** (on by default, gated by `Settings.updateCheck`). On startup Editora checks GitHub for a newer release, throttled to once/day and to once/session across windows. Pure, unit-tested **`update/UpdateCheck`** (java.base + Jackson `readTree` only): `parseLatest(mapper, json)` maps a GitHub `/releases/latest` payload ‚Üí `update/ReleaseInfo{version,url,name}` (strips a leading `v` via `normalizeVersion`; returns null for a `draft`/`prerelease` or a missing `tag_name`, never throws), `isNewer(current, latest)` (delegates to the shared `plugin/PluginInstaller.compareVersions`, so `0.10 > 0.9` numerically; a `0.0.0` dev fallback surfaces the real latest), and `isDue(lastCheckMs, nowMs, intervalMs)` (the once/day throttle; a future timestamp = clock-moved-back also counts as due). The impure **`update/UpdateService`** (the `GitService`/`PluginRegistry` idiom: one `update-check` daemon executor + `Platform.runLater`) HTTPS-GETs `AppInfo.LATEST_RELEASE_API` reusing `PluginRegistry.readCapped`/`isHttps` (bounded 1 MB; a `User-Agent` header ‚Äî GitHub 403s a missing one), parses via `UpdateCheck`, and posts an `Outcome{available, latest, error}`. **`AppInfo`** gained `GITHUB_REPO`/`LATEST_RELEASE_API`/`RELEASES_PAGE`. **`MainController`** owns the wiring: `maybeCheckForUpdates()` at the end of `init` (guarded by a static `updateCheckStartedThisSession` so only the first window hits the network, and `UpdateCheck.isDue` off the persisted `Settings.lastUpdateCheckEpoch`, which it stamps `now` before checking so a failed check doesn't retry all day); `onUpdateOutcome(outcome, manual)` caches a newer release in a **static `latestKnownUpdate`** (shared in-process so a second window + the About dialog see it) and `refreshUpdateNotice()`s; the notice is a **status-bar segment** (`StatusBar.setUpdateAvailable`, the `.status-update` accent pill, an `update.openDownloadPage` click target ‚Äî always shown even in Simple mode) gated on `latestKnownUpdate != null && version != Settings.dismissedUpdateVersion`. Commands: `help.checkForUpdates` (manual ‚Äî ignores the throttle *and* the setting, echoes checking/up-to-date/failed status), `update.openDownloadPage` (opens the release page ‚Äî `ReleaseInfo.url()`, else `AppInfo.RELEASES_PAGE` ‚Äî **and dismisses that version** by persisting `Settings.dismissedUpdateVersion`, hiding the segment), `view.toggleUpdateCheck`. `SettingsWindow.showAbout(...)` gained a nullable `ReleaseInfo` param ‚Üí an "Update available: X.Y.Z" link row. Settings ‚Üí Workspace ‚Üí **Updates** checkbox (+ a "contacts GitHub over HTTPS, sends no data" note). `Settings.updateCheck`/`lastUpdateCheckEpoch`/`dismissedUpdateVersion` (schema 76‚Üí77 additive √ó3). i18n √ó6 (`command.*`/`statusbar.update`/`statusbar.tip.update`/`settings.checkForUpdates`/`settings.section.updates`/`settings.updates.note`/`about.updateAvailable`/`status.update.*`; the `{0}`-parameterized ones avoid apostrophes for MessageFormat). **No new dependency / `module-info` change** (`java.net.http` + Jackson already required; the `update` package needs no `exports`/`opens` ‚Äî it reads JSON via `readTree`, no reflection). *Deferred: in-app download/auto-update (installers are unsigned), pre-release opt-in, a periodic re-check while running (only checks at startup), per-OS installer asset deep-linking.*
- **Markdown editing** (pure cores in `markdown/`, UI/overlays in `editor/`) ‚Äî an IntelliJ-style **selection format bar** + smart editing, gated to Markdown buffers (`isMarkdown()` + editable + non-huge + view mode ‚âÝ pure PREVIEW). Pure, unit-tested cores (no toolkit) all return a `markdown/MarkdownEdit` record (`from,to,replacement,selStart,selEnd`, applied via `area.replaceText`+`selectRange`, mirroring `Commenter`): **`MarkdownInline`** (toggle wrap/unwrap of `**`/`*`/`~~`/`` ` ``; `link(...)`; `linkAround(caret)` for open-link), **`MarkdownLines`** (`continuation(line)`/`isEmptyItem`/`markerLength` for list/quote continuation + `toggleBullet`), **`MarkdownHeading`** (`apply(delta)` promote/demote + `setLevel`, clamped 0‚Äì6, multi-line), **`MarkdownTable`** (`blockBounds(caret)` ‚Äî **no `Math.max(0,caret-1)` clamp**: `lastIndexOf` searches from *and including* `fromIndex`, so clamping caret 0 finds a leading `\n` and yields `substring(1,0)`, and this runs on every Enter/Tab in a Markdown buffer ‚Äî + `reflow` padding/aligning pipes honoring `:--`/`:-:`/`--:`; **an escaped `\|` is content, not a separator** ‚Äî cells are held *unescaped* inside the class and re-escaped on emit (`escapePipes`), widths are measured on the escaped form, and `cellIndexAt`/`cellContentOffset` skip escaped pipes, so a `fromCsv` table survives a Tab; plus **table generation/editing** ‚Äî `generate(rowsTotal, cols)` builds an aligned skeleton, `addRow`/`deleteRow`/`addColumn`/`deleteColumn` and `setAlignment(‚Ä¶, Align)` mutate the caret's table, each returning a `Nav{block,caret}` the controller applies like `tab`; the existing `tab`/`enter` give Tab-to-next-cell + add-row-on-Enter); `MarkdownLines.toggleTask` adds/removes a GFM checkbox (`- [ ] `). The **`editor/MarkdownFormatBar`** is a non-focus-traversable, free-positioned HBox of **icon buttons** ‚Äî the same `MenuIcons` glyphs the editor right-click menu uses (bold/italic/strikethrough/code/link) plus bullet-list, **task-list/checkbox**, and an **insert-table** grid button (`MenuIcons.bulletList()`/`taskList()`/`table()`) and a Normal/H1‚ÄìH6 `ComboBox` ‚Äî calling back into `EditorBuffer` format methods (icons instead of letter labels keep it consistent with the menu and avoid the barely-slanted italic "I"; kept in `editor`, no `ui` dependency, like `CompletionPopup`). `EditorBuffer` owns the lifecycle: a **coalesced** `selectionProperty`/scroll listener (`scheduleFormatBar`/`updateFormatBar`, pending-flag per pulse ‚Äî the `scheduleBraceMatch` idiom) positions it above the selection via `getCharacterBoundsOnScreen`‚Üí`screenToLocal`‚Üí`resizeRelocate` on `root`/`root2` (the ghost-label technique), hiding on Escape/blur/empty selection; format methods (`formatInline`/`formatLink`/`formatLinkFromClipboard`/`formatHeading`/`setHeadingLevel`/`formatBulletList`/`reflowTable`/`openLinkUnderCaret`) apply the core's `MarkdownEdit`; list/quote continuation lives in the existing `addAutoIndent` Enter filter; Ctrl/Cmd-click opens a link via an injected `setOpenUrlHandler` (controller `openExternalUrl`). Commands (markdown-gated, no-op elsewhere with a status): `markdown.bold`/`italic`/`strikethrough`/`code`/`link`/`bulletList`/`taskList`/`headingPromote`/`headingDemote`/`openLink`/`reflowTable`/`toggleFormatBar` + the table commands `insertTable` (the **mouse** path ‚Äî the format-bar button + right-click "Insert Table" ‚Äî opens a Typora/Word-style grid size-picker overlay; the **command-palette** path is keyboard-only, prompting for an `RxC` string parsed by the pure `MarkdownTable.parseSize`; both ‚Üí `EditorBuffer.insertTable`)/`tableAddRow`/`tableDeleteRow`/`tableAddColumn`/`tableDeleteColumn`/`tableAlignLeft`/`tableAlignCenter`/`tableAlignRight`, with Emacs `markdown-mode`-style chords (`C-c C-s b/i/s/c`, `C-c C-s u`/`k` (bullet/task list), `C-c C-a l`, `C-c C-h p|d`, `C-c C-o`, `C-c C-s t` ‚Äî note `C-c C-t` is taken by `view.toggleFold`) + a right-click **Format** group (`EditorBuffer.markdownMenuItems`, which also carries a **Table** submenu ‚Äî insert/add/delete row & column/align). Gated by `Settings.markdownFormatBar` (default on; schema 13‚Üí14 additive-identity; Settings ‚Üí Editor ‚Üí Markdown checkbox + `SettingsWindow.syncMarkdownFormatBarCheck`; `MainController.applyViewSettings` pushes `setFormatBarEnabled`). CSS `.markdown-format-bar`/`.md-fmt-*` in `app.css`; i18n `command.markdown.*`/`tooltip.markdown.*`/`markdown.heading.*`/`settings.markdownFormatBar`/`status.markdown.*` across the six catalogs. **No new dependency / `module-info` change.** The pure Markdown logic ‚Äî the editing cores (`MarkdownEdit`/`MarkdownInline`/`MarkdownLines`/`MarkdownHeading`/`MarkdownTable`), the lint cores (`MarkdownLint`/`MarkdownLintConfig`/`MarkdownLintDirectives`/`MarkdownLintFix` ‚Äî MD009 exempts a **hard line break** via the shared `MarkdownLint.isHardLineBreak` (exactly 2 trailing spaces before a non-blank line = `<br>`, allowed by upstream's `br_spaces: 2`; the fixer must use the same rule or it deletes the break)), `MarkdownOutline`, and `MarkdownImagePaste` ‚Äî lives in its own **`com.editora.markdown`** package (internal, no `exports`/`opens`/`module-info` change), with their unit tests under `com.editora.markdown`; the FX `MarkdownRenderer`, the preview/lint overlays + stripes, `MarkdownFormatBar`, and the image loaders (`PreviewImageLoader`/`MermaidImages`/`MathImages`) stay in `editor/` as the editor's rendering surfaces.  Tables also convert to/from **CSV**: pure/unit-tested `MarkdownTable.fromCsv` (delimiter auto-detect comma/semicolon/tab, RFC-4180 quoting, pipe-escaping) and `toCsv` back the GFM table block to the clipboard, via `EditorBuffer.tableFromCsv`/`tableToCsv` ‚Üí commands `markdown.tableFromCsv`/`markdown.tableToCsv` + the right-click Table submenu. The caret's table also **file-exports** to **CSV / Excel (`.xlsx`) / ODF (`.ods`)**: `EditorBuffer.exportTableFile(format)` renders the table via `MarkdownTable.toCsv` then hands the CSV + format to the injected `setTableFileExporter` (editor stays free of `ui`/`office`); `MainController.exportMarkdownTableFile` picks the destination (`chooseOfficeDestination`) and either writes the CSV text (`exportCsvTextToFile`) or reuses the CSV grid's `csvExportSpreadsheet` (`CsvParser.parse` ‚Üí `office/OfficeExportService.exportXlsx`/`exportOds`, header row = true since `toCsv` drops the `---` divider). Commands `markdown.tableExportCsv`/`tableExportExcel`/`tableExportOds` (palette + the right-click Table submenu, `MenuIcons.download()`); no new dependency.  **Table of contents:** pure/unit-tested `markdown/MarkdownToc` (`build`/`updated`/`slug`, reusing `MarkdownOutline.headings`) generates a nested list of GitHub-anchor heading links; `EditorBuffer.insertOrUpdateToc` inserts it wrapped in `<!-- toc -->`/`<!-- /toc -->` markers at the caret, or regenerates the existing marker block in place ‚Äî command `markdown.toc` (palette + the right-click Markdown menu). (Supersedes the registry `markdown-toc` plugin.) **Image insertion** (pure `markdown/MarkdownImagePaste`: `uniqueFileName`/`relativePath`/`snippet`/`imageUrlFromDrag`/`extensionForUrl`): pasting a clipboard image (`tryMarkdownImagePaste`), dropping image **files** (`EditorBuffer.installImageDrop` ‚Üí `MainController.insertDroppedImages`), and dragging a **raw image / image URL out of a web browser** (`setWebImageDropHandler` ‚Üí `insertWebImage`) all copy/download the bytes into a sibling `assets/` dir and insert `![](assets/‚Ä¶)`. The browser path resolves the source via `MarkdownImagePaste.imageUrlFromDrag` (drag URL ‚Üí `<img src>` in the dragged HTML ‚Üí an image-looking string) and downloads it **off the FX thread** (`PreviewImageLoader.fetchBytes`, handling http(s) + `data:`); a raw `Dragboard` image is encoded to PNG via `PreviewImageLoader.imageToPng` (headless Java2D, no `javafx.swing`); on total failure it falls back to inserting the remote URL. Requires a saved local file (`assets/` resolves next to it; else `status.markdown.imageNeedsSave`). *Deferred: reference-style links, WYSIWYG inline rendering, table auto-format-on-type, table cell-merge / move-row-or-column, format bar in plaintext.*
- **Personal Notes** ‚Äî file-attached annotations stored **outside** the file (for read-only/generated/shared code), built as a *separate* feature that reuses the **Bookmarks** machinery (see the bookmarks paragraph) rather than extending it; the two coexist. **Model** (`config/`, all Jackson-serialized so they ride the existing `opens com.editora.config to jackson.databind` ‚Äî no `module-info` change): `enum NoteScope{WORD,LINE,RANGE}`, `enum NoteStatus{ACTIVE,RESOLVED,ORPHANED}`, `record FileIdentity(path,canonicalPath,size,lastModified,hash)` (pure `of(Path)` sha-256 capped at `MAX_HASH_BYTES`=5 MB, pure `match(a,b)` priority **canonicalPath ‚Üí contentHash ‚Üí similarPath**. **A content-hash match is not identity** ‚Äî `PathKeys.findKeyByIdentity` (the re-key used when a buffer's path key misses) trusts it only when the candidate's own file is **gone from disk** (injected `Predicate<String> stillExists`, so it stays pure), because two files can hold the same bytes (`cp x x.bak`, a duplicated LICENSE, a monorepo's boilerplate `index.ts`) and accepting the hash alone made *opening* such a file `remove` the other's notes and re-`put` them under the new key ‚Äî deleting them from the original), `record TextAnchor(line,column,endLine,endColumn,selectedText,prefix,suffix)` (`MAX_TEXT`/`MAX_CONTEXT` caps), `record PersonalNote(UUID id, FileIdentity, NoteScope, TextAnchor, body, List<String> tags, NoteStatus, long createdAt, long updatedAt)` ‚Äî **`long` epoch-millis timestamps deliberately** (the default `ObjectMapper` has no jsr310 module). `NoteStore` mirrors `BookmarkStore`: `schemaVersion` + per-project `Map<projectKey, Map<fileKey, List<PersonalNote>>> byProject` (fileKey = canonicalPath), static `mergePreservingOrder(prev,current)` (matches by note **id**). **Storage**: a single versioned `notes.json` (`ConfigManager.getNotesFile`/`getNotes()` = the active project's bucket via the same `currentBookmarkKey()` derivation as bookmarks / `saveNotes()` / `loadNotes()` via `ConfigMigrations.readVersioned(..., ConfigSchema.NOTES)` / `deleteNotesForProject`), kept out of `WorkspaceState` like bookmarks. **Anchoring** (`editor/`): pure, unit-tested `NoteAnchors` (`shiftOffset`/`shiftRange` interval-adjust through a `PlainTextChange`; `relocate(doc,savedStart,savedEnd,selectedText,prefix,suffix)` ‚Üí `int[]{start,end}` or null=orphan: level-1 exact-offset check, else occurrence scoring with a prefix/suffix-context bonus + proximity, bounded by `MAX_OCCURRENCES`). `NoteManager` (per-buffer, like `BookmarkManager`): holds `Map<UUID,Tracked>` of notes + live offset ranges, subscribes to `area.plainTextChanges()` to shift ranges (does **not** fire `onChanged` on edit-shifts ‚Äî only `onLinesRepaint`; persistence happens on save/tab-switch, never per-keystroke), exposes `isNoted(line)`/`notesOnLine`/`noteAt(offset)`/`activeLines`/`next`/`previous`/`activeSpans()` (for the overlay), `add/update/remove/setStatus/clear` (these fire `onChanged`), `snapshot()` (rebuilds anchors from offsets), and `restore(saved)` (relocates each via `NoteAnchors`, returns whether anything moved/orphaned so the controller self-heal-persists ‚Äî the bookmark pattern). **Editor surface**: `NoteHighlightOverlay` (a mouse-transparent `Canvas` mirroring `SpellCheckOverlay`/`WhitespaceOverlay`: coalesced per-pulse redraw, visible-spans only, soft amber wash) paints behind each note's anchored span as a **flat, contiguous fill drawn like a text selection** (`paintSpan`, clamped to `first/lastVisibleParToAllParIndex`): one square fillRect **per visible line** with no per-line outline/rounding so adjacent lines join seamlessly; intermediate lines of a multi-line range fill to the viewport's right edge (matching how a selection paints the included line break), the first line starts at the start column and the last line stops at the end column; it also draws a small **amber corner-triangle marker at the note's start character** (inline, on the note's first visible line) ‚Äî the "there's a note here" indicator is now inline at the selection start, **not** a gutter slot, and is **clickable** (`EditorBuffer.setNoteMarkerClick` ‚Üí edit the note ‚Äî restoring the old gutter click-to-edit). A `mouse-moved` hover (guarded to only update when the hovered note id changes) shows the body in a `Tooltip` whose graphic is the body **rendered as Markdown** (`renderNoteTooltip` ‚Üí `MarkdownRenderer`, in the editor's own font family/size, with `app.css`+`syntax.css` attached to the node since the tooltip lives in its own popup scene; plain-label fallback on failure); the editor right-click menu prepends "Add Personal Note"/"Add Note to Selection" (when `path != null`). `EditorBuffer` mirrors the bookmark API: `getNoteManager`, `setAddNoteHandler`, `setOnNotesChanged`, `applyNotes`, `captureNoteDraft()` (infers WORD/RANGE/LINE + prefix/suffix context), `fileIdentity()`, `setNoteIndicatorsVisible`. **UI/commands**: `NotesPanel` (a `ToolWindowContent` modeled on `BookmarksPanel`) groups notes per file with a filter (bold file-header rows like Find-in-Files, plus a trailing clear-(`‚úï`) button shown only while the filter has text, reusing `.project-filter-bar`/`.project-filter-clear`), NoteCell context menu (Edit/Resolve‚ÜîReopen/Delete, file: Delete all), double-click/Enter to open; tool window id `notes` (`tool.notes`, `M-5`, `Icons.notes()`). **`ui/NotesCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` feature-coordinator pattern) owns the `NotesPanel` + the two cross-file pickers + `persistNotes`/`restoreNotes` (run on save / tab switch / project switch; re-key by hash when the path key misses but the bucket is non-empty), `addNoteFromContext`/`addNoteAtCaret`, `editNoteAtCaret` (the `notes.editNote` command ‚Äî edit the note at the caret, replacing the old gutter-click), `jumpNote` (next/previous), the `notes.jump` cross-file QuickOpen (`M-g n` ‚Äî matches the note's first line) + `searchNotes` (`notes.search` ‚Äî the same picker but its `QuickOpen` `searchKey` matches the **full body + tags + file** via `noteSearchText`, while the displayed label stays the first line; `QuickOpen` gained an optional `searchKey` ctor arg defaulting to the label, so other pickers are unchanged), `deleteNoteAtCaret`, `exportNotes` (FileChooser ‚Üí JSON), the `showNoteDialog` editor, and the gating (`applySupport`/`ifEnabled`/`migrateKey`); it reaches the window via the shared host plus a small `Ops` extension (open-path / navigate-to-line / the shared `noteKey` + open-buffer-for-key / install-emacs-keys / tool-window availability / the `notes.json` map). `MainController` keeps the `ToolWindow` (built with `notesCoordinator.panel()`), the global `promptText`/`noteKey`/`tabForKey`/`navigateToLine`/`openPath` helpers, the rename-migration call (`notesCoordinator.migrateKey`), and wires `addBuffer`'s note hooks + the `notes.*`/`view.toggleNotes` commands to the coordinator. (Resolve/Reopen is available from the panel's NoteCell menu; there's no caret command for it.) Bodies are edited via `showNoteDialog(initial, onAccept, onDelete)` ‚Äî a **multi-line** `TextArea` `Dialog` (Enter = newline, Ctrl/Cmd+Enter = save) with the user's **configured keybindings** installed for caret movement + basic editing via `command/TextInputKeymap.install(textArea, keymap)` (a dialog has its own scene, so the global `KeyDispatcher` isn't there ‚Äî `TextInputKeymap` adds a `KEY_PRESSED` filter that resolves the same chord token through `KeymapManager` and runs the matching `nav.*`/`edit.*` action on the `TextInputControl`, e.g. Emacs `C-a`/`C-e`/`C-f`/`C-b`/`C-n`/`C-p`/`M-f`/`M-b`/`C-d`/`C-k`/`C-w`/`M-w`/`C-y`; pure caret math `lineStart`/`lineEnd`/`lineUp`/`lineDown`/`backToIndentation` is unit-tested; reusable for any dialog text field); when editing an existing note it shows a left-aligned **Delete** button (`onDelete`) that **confirms first** (a native `CONFIRMATION` alert). The dialog also shows a muted hint (`.note-dialog-hint`) that the body supports **Markdown** (it renders as Markdown in the hover tooltip). `promptNoteBody` delegates to it with no delete. Commands: `notes.add` (`C-c n`), `notes.editNote` (`C-c e`, edit the note at the caret ‚Äî also via clicking the inline marker), `notes.toggleResolved` (resolve/reopen the note at the caret), `notes.next`/`previous`, `notes.jump` (`M-g n`), `notes.search` (`M-g s`, full-text picker), `notes.delete` (deletes the note on the caret line; also in the panel + the editor's Delete button), `notes.export`, `tool.notes` (`M-5`). **Gated by `Settings.notesSupport`** ("Enable Personal Notes", Settings ‚Üí Application, default **on**) ‚Äî `NotesCoordinator.applySupport()` (mirrors `GitCoordinator.applySupport`, called at init + on every settings apply) hides the Notes tool window (`toolWindows.setAvailable`), sets each buffer's `setNotesEnabled` (gates the editor "Add Note" menu items), and on the off‚Üíon transition `restoreNotes` every open buffer; the `ifEnabled(...)` wrapper no-ops each `notes.*`/`tool.notes` command + keybinding, those ids are filtered from the command palette, and `persistNotes`/`restoreNotes` early-return while off. A second **view toggle** `Settings.showNoteIndicators` (default on, only effective when notes are enabled) hides just the inline start marker + highlight ‚Äî `applyViewSettings` applies the effective `notesSupport && showNoteIndicators`, and the Settings "Show note indicators" checkbox disables when the master is off (autocomplete master/sub pattern). All strings localized in the six catalogs. *Deferred: fuzzy match beyond nearest-text, scrollbar/minimap markers, Markdown note bodies, team/cloud sync ‚Äî the model already carries tags/status/FileIdentity so these are additive.*
- `vfs/` ‚Äî **Remote file access (SFTP)**. Edit/browse/search files on a remote host over SSH/SFTP. The
  approach keeps `EditorBuffer.path` a `java.nio.file.Path` but lets it belong to a **non-default
  filesystem** (a MINA SSHD `SftpFileSystem`), so `Files.readString`/`writeString`/`list`/`walkFileTree`/
  `readAttributes` keep working over SFTP and the Project tree / search / open / save need no rewrite. The
  only local-only boundary is `path.toFile()` (used by `ProcessRunner`/LSP/DAP/run) ‚Äî gated off for remote.
  **`Vfs`** (pure, unit-tested) is the seam: `isLocal(Path)` (= `path.getFileSystem() == FileSystems.getDefault()`,
  the single predicate every local-process feature gates on; a null/untitled path counts as local),
  `toStorableString`/`parseStorable` (a path‚Üîstring round-trip ‚Äî local plain, remote as its `sftp://` URI,
  reconstructed through an injected resolver), `isRemoteUri`, `displayLabel`. **`SftpUri`** (pure,
  unit-tested) parses/formats `sftp://[user@]host[:port]/path` and yields the `authority()` connection key.
  **`RemoteConnection`** (record: host/port/user/`AuthMethod {DEFAULT_KEYS, KEY, PASSWORD}`/keyPath/label/
  lastPath ‚Äî **no secret**) + **`config/ConnectionStore`** (schema-versioned `connections.json`,
  `ConfigSchema.CONNECTIONS`; `ConfigManager.getConnections`/`putConnection`/`removeConnection`/
  `saveConnections`/`loadConnections`). **`RemoteFileSystems`** (UI-owned, the `GitService` idiom: a daemon
  executor + `Platform.runLater`) holds one `SftpFileSystem` per `user@host:port`, `connect(conn, secret,
  cb)` (auth precedence **default `~/.ssh` keys ‚Üí key file ‚Üí password**; the secret `char[]` is wiped after
  use, and the password is removed from the SSH session the instant the handshake finishes ‚Äî
  `RemoteFileSystems.authenticate`'s `finally` ‚Äî so MINA's String-only `addPasswordIdentity` copy isn't
  retained on the session for the whole connection), `pathFor(SftpUri)`/`disconnect`/`shutdown`, and wires `Vfs.setRemoteResolver` so remote URIs in
  recent-files reconstruct to live Paths. **Local-only gating** (all inert for local files, so zero
  behavior change): `MainController.isLocalBuffer` + `Vfs.isLocal` guards on LSP (`syncBufferLsp`
  eligibility), DAP/breakpoints (`isDebuggableBuffer`), run/shell-run/HTTP (`addBuffer`), git
  (`refreshGit` ‚Üí `RepoState.NONE` for a remote context), and external-change polling
  (`checkExternalChanges` skips remote ‚Äî a network `mtime` per focus). **Remote stays text-capable**:
  editing, highlighting, search, bookmarks, notes, preview, PDF/print. **The SFTP UI/commands live in
  `ui/RemoteCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` feature-coordinator pattern ‚Äî owns the `RemoteFileSystems`
  engine + the `RemoteConnectionsPanel` + the mount state, reaching the window via the shared host plus an
  `Ops` extension for keymap / open-path / set-project-root / open-project-tool-window / active-project-root /
  error-report (reusing `GitCoordinator.gitError`) / the `connections.json` get/put/remove; `MainController`
  keeps the `remote` `ToolWindow` built with `remoteCoordinator.panel()`, queries `isMounted()` for the
  current-folder view, and wires the `remote.*`/`tool.remote` commands + the Welcome quick-connect to it).
  **UI/commands**:
  `remote.connect` (an `OverlayInput` form ‚Äî host/port/user/auth + key Browse/secret/path, localized auth
  picker; on success **mounts the remote folder as the Project tree root** via `projectPanel.setRoot` +
  opens the Project tool window, and `config.putConnection`s it), `remote.manageConnections` (a `QuickOpen`
  over saved connections ‚Üí re-opens the form pre-filled), `remote.openFile` (an `sftp://` URI ‚Üí
  `Vfs.parseStorable` ‚Üí `openPath`), `remote.disconnect` (restores the local project root). **Saved sites get
  three visible surfaces** (all over the same `connections.json` most-recent-first list ‚Äî no schema/secret
  change): a **Remote Sites tool window** (`ui/RemoteConnectionsPanel`, id `remote`, `Side.RIGHT`, `Icons::remote`,
  `tool.remote`/`M-g r`, *not* buffer-gated, **registered default-hidden** via `toolWindows.register(tw, false)` ‚Äî
  the stripe button is off until the user enables it (Settings ‚Üí Tool Windows or `tool.remote`), and it opens on the
  right; the remote *functionality* is unaffected ‚Äî a flat `ListView` of saved sites; double-click/Enter or the
  New/Connect/Remove bar ‚Üí `connectRemote(c)`/`removeConnection`/`connectRemote()`, refreshed on open + after a
  mount); a **Settings ‚Üí Remote master-detail page** (`SettingsWindow.remoteConnectionsEditor`, mirroring the
  External Tools page ‚Äî list + label/host/port/user/auth/key-path form editing the immutable `RemoteConnection`
  record via `remoteItems.set(i, ‚Ä¶)`, persisted through the new `ConfigManager.setConnections(list)` ‚Üí
  `SharedConfig` whole-list replace; opened by `remote.settings` ‚Üí `showRemote`); and a **Welcome-page "Remote
  Sites" quick-connect list** (`WelcomePane.remoteList`, shown only when non-empty, each row ‚Üí `connectRemote(c)`).
  All three open the **prefilled connect form** on pick (so the secret is still prompted), never a silent
  reconnect. A remote buffer
  opens with a remote `Path`, so plain Save ‚Üí `writeBuffer` ‚Üí `Files.writeString` writes back over SFTP, no
  dialog; `saveAs` is guarded for remote. Recent files round-trip the `sftp://` URI (`Vfs.toStorableString`;
  a remote entry resolves only once its connection is open). **Host-key verification (do not weaken):** the client uses a `KnownHostsServerKeyVerifier` over **`~/.ssh/known_hosts`** ‚Äî shared with OpenSSH on purpose. Unknown host ‚Üí the injected `RemoteFileSystems.HostKeyPrompt` (trust-on-first-use; `RemoteCoordinator` marshals it to FX and blocks the SSH I/O thread, bounded + fail-closed), written to the file only on acceptance; **changed key ‚Üí refused without asking** (that's the MITM ‚Äî a prompt there just gets clicked through); no prompt ‚Üí refuse. It shipped as `AcceptAllServerKeyVerifier`, which made every SFTP session unauthenticated and handed a password-auth MITM the password (GHSA-p4qf-p7q6-2mrw). Tested against a real in-process `SshServer` **and a real impostor on the same port** (`HostKeyVerificationTest` + `RemoteFileSystemsHostKeyFxTest`); the known_hosts path is ctor-injectable so tests never touch the real one. **Dependency:** Apache **MINA SSHD**
  (`org.apache.sshd:sshd-osgi` + `sshd-sftp`) ‚Äî the combined **sshd-osgi** bundle (module
  `org.apache.sshd.osgi`) is used instead of sshd-common+sshd-core, which **split** the
  `org.apache.sshd.common`/`server` packages across two automatic modules (illegal under JPMS); `sshd-sftp`
  **excludes** sshd-core/sshd-common + **`jcl-over-slf4j`** (its `org.apache.commons.logging` module
  collides with pdfbox's commons-logging under jlink), and **slf4j-api is forced to 2.0.17** (a real
  module, not the automatic 1.7.36 SSHD pins). `module-info` `requires org.apache.sshd.osgi`/`.sftp` +
  `opens com.editora.vfs to com.fasterxml.jackson.databind` (the `RemoteConnection` record). **dist/jlink
  moditect:** sshd-osgi uses a hand-maintained `src/moditect/module-info-sshd-osgi.java` (jdeps's 106
  exports + a `requires org.slf4j` jdeps drops under `--ignore-missing-deps` ‚Äî without it every SSHD class
  fails at load), and sshd-sftp uses a hand-written client-only `<moduleInfoSource>` (drops the unused SFTP-
  *server* `SubsystemFactory` provides that jlink rejects, keeps only the nio FileSystemProvider). The
  `-Pdist` app-image builds, links, and launches. *Deferred: OS-keychain secret storage + auto-reconnect on
  launch, true ssh-agent (SSH_AUTH_SOCK), remote LSP/DAP/git/run, remote Save-As / new-file, a status-bar
  remote indicator + tab tooltip, remote-search caps, FTP/WebDAV/cloud providers (the layer generalizes).*
- `plugin/` ‚Äî **Plugin support** (off by default, gated by `Settings.pluginSupport`; **also off in Simple UI
  mode** via `pluginsEnabled()`). A plugin is a folder `<configDir>/plugins/<id>/` with a `plugin.json`
  manifest + optionally a Java jar (`*.jar`/`lib/*.jar`) + `snippets/`/`templates/` dirs. **The one hard
  constraint:** the `-Pdist` build is a **sealed jlink image with no module path at runtime** and there is no
  `ServiceLoader` infra, so plugins are discovered by **manifest** and a Java plugin's classes load via a
  child **`URLClassLoader(jarUrls, appClassLoader)`** (parent = the app module's loader ‚Üí the plugin can use
  Editora's **exported** packages `com.editora.plugin`/`command`/`ui`/`editor`/`config` + the baked JDK/JavaFX
  modules via normal parent delegation; **no `ModuleLayer`**). Compile a plugin on a plain **classpath**, not
  the module path. **API (the exported `com.editora.plugin` package):** `interface Plugin {void start(ctx);
  default void stop()}`; `interface PluginContext` (`registerCommand(id,title,Runnable)`, `bindKey(chord,
  commandId)`, `registerToolWindow(id,title,ToolWindowSide,Region,commandId[,Supplier<Node> icon])` (the icon
  overload sets the stripe glyph ‚Äî a `Supplier<javafx.scene.Node>`, e.g. an `SVGPath` with the `toolbar-icon`
  style class; the no-icon overload is a `default` delegating with `null` ‚áí the jigsaw `Icons.plugin()`),
  `addEditorMenuItem(label,
  Consumer<ActiveEditor>)`, `addStatusBarSegment(label,commandId)`, `activeEditor()`, `pluginDir()/dataDir()/
  configDir()`, `log/setStatus`); `interface ActiveEditor` (narrow editor facade ‚Äî `filePath/text/
  selectedText/replaceSelection/insertAtCaret/setText/openPath` (`setText` = whole-buffer replace, undoable ‚Äî
  for whole-file transforms like formatting), **never** exposes `MainController`); `enum
  ToolWindowSide{LEFT,RIGHT,BOTTOM}` (keeps the API package free of a hard `ui` dependency); lenient Jackson
  `PluginManifest` (`@JsonIgnoreProperties` ‚Äî `id/name/version/main`, `Map keymap`, `List<DeclaredCommand>
  commands{id,title,List<String> run,dir}`) + `PluginDescriptor` (manifest/dir/enabled/classLoader/loadError).
  **`PluginManager`** is **shared, owned by `ui/WindowManager`** (created once with `(pluginsDir, isEnabled
  predicate)` + `discover()`): `discover()` scans the dir, parses each manifest (`parseManifest`, unit-tested),
  builds one `URLClassLoader` per enabled Java plugin; `instantiate(descriptor)` does `Class.forName(main,...)`
  + `newInstance` under the plugin TCCL, catching `Throwable` ‚Üí null (one bad plugin never blocks others).
  **The whole plugin feature lives in `ui/PluginCoordinator`** (the `CoordinatorHost` pattern): it owns the
  per-window `PluginRegistry`/`PluginInstaller`, the started-plugin instances, the plugin-contributed tool
  windows + editor menu items, the "Browse Plugins" picker, and the two inner adapters
  (`PluginContextImpl`/`ActiveEditorImpl`). The shared `PluginManager` (owned by `WindowManager`) is passed
  in; `MainController` keeps the `pluginManager` field + thin `disposePlugins()` (the `WindowManager`
  window-close contract) and `pluginsEnabled()` delegates, and wires `applyPlugins` / the buffer-gating
  (`gateToolWindows`) / the editor-menu contributor (`editorMenuItems`) / the `plugins.*`+`view.togglePlugins`
  commands to the coordinator; `PluginCoordinator.pluginCapabilitySummary` is the public static the Settings
  page also calls. **Multi-window:** classes load **once** (shared manager), but a `Plugin` **instance + its
  tool-window content Node are built per window** (a Node can't live in two scenes) ‚Äî `PluginCoordinator.applyPlugins()` (run in
  `init`, **before** `toolWindows.restore()` so contributed windows restore their visibility) registers the
  declarative bits + `plugin.<id>.<cmd>` external commands (`runDeclaredCommand` ‚Üí `process/ProcessRunner`
  off-thread) + applies the shared `keymap.applyOverrides(manifest.keymap)`, then `instantiate` + `start(new
  PluginContextImpl(d))` each Java plugin; `disposePlugins()` (window close) calls each `stop()`.
  `PluginContextImpl.fullId(id)` namespaces a bare command/tool-window id to `plugin.<id>.<...>` (a dotted id
  = a built-in, used verbatim); tool windows register via `toolWindows.register` + a toggle command,
  status-bar segments via `StatusBar.addPluginSegment`, editor menu items via a `setMenuContributor` hook on
  each `EditorBuffer` (the `editor` package stays decoupled ‚Äî a `Supplier<List<MenuItem>>` injected from
  `MainController.pluginEditorMenuItems`). **Buffer-gated stripe:** every registered plugin tool window is
  tracked in `MainController.pluginToolWindows` and its stripe button is gated on an open editor buffer
  (`toolWindows.setAvailable(tw, activeBuffer() != null)` at registration + in `updateBufferToolWindows()`,
  alongside the built-in Structure/File-Info/TODO windows) ‚Äî plugins act on the active editor, so they're
  hidden on a non-buffer tab (e.g. Welcome). **Opt-out:** the full
  `registerToolWindow(id,title,side,content,commandId,icon,needsBuffer)` overload takes a `needsBuffer` flag
  (the icon/no-icon overloads are `default`s delegating with `true`); a plugin passes `false` for a
  self-contained tool window (scratchpad/calculator/‚Ä¶) so it's **not** added to `pluginToolWindows` and stays
  available on every tab. Declarative **assets**: `SnippetManager.addExtraSourceDir`/
  `TemplateRegistry.addExtraSourceDir` (generalized extra-source-dir lists, cache-clearing) merge a plugin's
  `snippets/`/`templates/` into the registries (`reload()`d once after applying). **Enabled set** lives in
  `<configDir>/plugins.json` (`config/PluginStore`, schema-versioned via `ConfigSchema.PLUGINS`, owned by
  `SharedConfig` ‚Äî `getPluginStore`/`savePlugins`/`getPluginsDir`). **Gating:** `Settings.pluginSupport`
  (default off; schema 21‚Üí22 additive-identity) + `applyPlugins` early-returns when off, so `plugin.*`
  commands are never even registered when disabled (no palette filter needed). **Settings ‚Üí Plugins** page
